package_gnu="no"; \
test -n "$package_gnu" || { \
  if { if (LC_ALL=C find --version) 2>/dev/null | grep GNU >/dev/null; then \
	 LC_ALL=C find -L .. -maxdepth 1 -type f \
		       -size -10000000c -exec grep 'GNU xz' \
		       /dev/null '{}' ';' 2>/dev/null; \
       else \
	 LC_ALL=C grep 'GNU xz' ../* 2>/dev/null; \
       fi; \
     } | grep -v 'libtool:' >/dev/null; then \
     package_gnu=yes; \
   else \
     package_gnu=no; \
   fi; \
}; \
if test "$package_gnu" = "yes"; then \
  package_prefix='GNU '; \
else \
  package_prefix=''; \
fi; \

test ! -f xz.po || { \
  if test -f ./xz.pot-header; then \
    sed -e '1,/^#$/d' < xz.po > xz.1po && \
    cat ./xz.pot-header xz.1po > xz.po; \
    rm -f xz.1po; \
  fi; \
  if test -f ./xz.pot; then \
    sed -f remove-potcdate.sed < ./xz.pot > xz.1po && \
    sed -f remove-potcdate.sed < xz.po > xz.2po && \
    if cmp xz.1po xz.2po >/dev/null 2>&1; then \
      rm -f xz.1po xz.2po xz.po; \
    else \
      rm -f xz.1po xz.2po ./xz.pot && \
      mv xz.po ./xz.pot; \
    fi; \
  else \
    mv xz.po ./xz.pot; \
  fi; \
}
